09 Mar 2017 20:55:03 : The Wild Weebs, general, Wertfuzzy77#0274, ```Parser
Turns a written document into a list of index-able terms.
Pro - Allows the text to be accessed and transformed easily
Con - Removes the words from context.

Stopping
Removes the common words
Pro - Makes your data smaller and easier to manage
Con - makes it impossible to search for something like "To be or Not to be" which may all be stop words

Stemming
Shortens words to allow for easier searching. Ex Running -> Run.  So searching for "Run" would be also find terms for "Running"
Pro - Allows for easier searching, and makes similar words into the same indexable search term
Con - Can be bad for other languages like Arabic, in which stemming causes more harm than it benefits.

Link Extraction and analysis
Extracts links and anchor text from the document
Pro - Useful for PageRank Algorithms and analysis for these links can be used to rank website popularity
Con - Can remove valuable index-able terms from the search. Ex. if you wanted to search for a site with a lot of youtube.com urls, and you searched for "youtube" it might not find those URLs in your index as they will be classified as links and be taken out from the index.

Information extraction
Extracts phrases or pairs of words that have meanings. Like Names or Bolded headings
Pro - Can make important or specific things easier to search for. Like searching for "Large Haldron Collider" would now find more specific things related to the particle accelerator, instead of searching for the individual terms 
Con - Can misinterpret phrases and it could also increase run time. 

Classifier
Classifies sections of the data in certain categories. Notably used to classify spam and advertising text. 
Pro - The search will be more accurate and will only include valuable data
Con - Important sections of text can be marked as spam

```
09 Mar 2017 20:55:52 : The Wild Weebs, general, Wertfuzzy77#0274, ```
S1Reader <- A Stream connecting to the file S1 is in
STOPWORDS = ['all', 'he', 'them']
Tokens <- a blank list # Since we have a small amount of words to parse, a list will work
WHILE S1Reader.hasMore() DO # Loops until we run out of words
    word = S1Reader.getNext() to lowercase # Gets the next word
    word <- word with all non-alphanumeric characters removed
    IF word not in STOPWORDS DO # Confirms that the word isnt a stop word
        IF length of word > 3 and the last character is 's' DO # Stems if necessary
            word <- word without the last character (The s)
        END IF
    append word to Tokens # Adds the word to the Token list
    END IF
END WHILE
return Tokens

Final Output
['as', 'john', 'like', 'chocolate', 'ate']

10 Mar 2017 07:50:42 : LimitlessMc, mainchat, Jay113355#4999, f.lux

f.lux fixes this: it makes the color of your computer's display adapt to the time of day, warm at night and like sunlight during the day.

It's even possible that you're staying up too late because of your computer. You could use f.lux because it makes you sleep better, or you could just use it just because it makes your computer look better.
